LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t."Id", t."CreatedDate", t."Discriminator", t."FileName", t."Path", t."StorageType", t."Showcase", p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId"
    FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
        FROM "Files" AS f
        WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
    ) AS t ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t."Id"
) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"

SELECT t."Id", t."CategoryId", t."CategoryId1", t."CreatedDate", t."Name", t."ProductId", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Name", t1."Price", t1."SubCategoryId", t1."SubCategoryId1", t1."UnitsInStock", t1."UpdatedDate", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId", t1."Id0", t1."CreatedDate0", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."Path", t1."StorageType", t1."Showcase"
FROM (
    SELECT s."Id", s."CategoryId", s."CategoryId1", s."CreatedDate", s."Name", s."ProductId", s."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "SubCategories" AS s
    WHERE s."Id" = @__Parse_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CreatedDate", p."Name", p."Price", p."SubCategoryId", p."SubCategoryId1", p."UnitsInStock", p."UpdatedDate", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId", t0."Id" AS "Id0", t0."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."Path", t0."StorageType", t0."Showcase"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."Path", t2."StorageType", t2."Showcase"
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."SubCategoryId1"
ORDER BY t."Id", t1."Id", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId"

FROM "SubCategories" AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CreatedDate", p."Name", p."Price", p."SubCategoryId", p."UnitsInStock", p."UpdatedDate", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId", t0."Id" AS "Id0", t0."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."Path", t0."StorageType", t0."Showcase"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t."Id", t."CreatedDate", t."Discriminator", t."FileName", t."Path", t."StorageType", t."Showcase"
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t."Id"
    ) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"
) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SubCategoryId"
ORDER BY s."Id", t1."Id", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId"

2023-03-29 22:54:57.595 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (35ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT s."Id", s."CategoryId", s."CreatedDate", s."Name", s."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Name", t1."Price", t1."SubCategoryId", t1."UnitsInStock", t1."UpdatedDate", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId", t1."Id0", t1."CreatedDate0", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."Path", t1."StorageType", t1."Showcase"
FROM "SubCategories" AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CreatedDate", p."Name", p."Price", p."SubCategoryId", p."UnitsInStock", p."UpdatedDate", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId", t0."Id" AS "Id0", t0."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."Path", t0."StorageType", t0."Showcase"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t."Id", t."CreatedDate", t."Discriminator", t."FileName", t."Path", t."StorageType", t."Showcase"
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t."Id"
    ) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"
) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SubCategoryId"
ORDER BY s."Id", t1."Id", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId"

SELECT s."Id", s."CategoryId", s."CreatedDate", s."Name", s."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Name", t1."Price", t1."SubCategoryId", t1."UnitsInStock", t1."UpdatedDate", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId", t1."Id0", t1."CreatedDate0", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."Path", t1."StorageType", t1."Showcase"
FROM "SubCategories" AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CreatedDate", p."Name", p."Price", p."SubCategoryId", p."UnitsInStock", p."UpdatedDate", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId", t0."Id" AS "Id0", t0."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."Path", t0."StorageType", t0."Showcase"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t."Id", t."CreatedDate", t."Discriminator", t."FileName", t."Path", t."StorageType", t."Showcase"
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t."Id"
    ) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"
) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SubCategoryId"
ORDER BY s."Id", t1."Id", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId"

FROM "SubCategories" AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p."Id", p."CreatedDate", p."Name", p."Price", p."SubCategoryId", p."UnitsInStock", p."UpdatedDate", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId", t0."Id" AS "Id0", t0."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."Path", t0."StorageType", t0."Showcase"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t."Id", t."CreatedDate", t."Discriminator", t."FileName", t."Path", t."StorageType", t."Showcase"
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."Path", f."StorageType", f."Showcase"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t."Id"
    ) AS t0 ON p."Id" = t0."ProductsId"
) AS t1 ON s."Id" = t1."SubCategoryId"
ORDER BY s."Id", t1."Id", t1."ProductImageFilesId", t1."ProductsId"
